After all that work, I couldn\u2019t not do the marathon. Up to mile 20 my plan worked perfectly. I took it easy. Everything felt fine. Then. It happened. Throbbing pain every time my left foot hit the ground. I had 6 miles to go. First, I just panicked. To set goals and accomplish them. \\n\\nI\u2019ll be back next year.
